Guangdong's Measures to Suppress the Silver Industry 80

Passed by the Provincial Government and Promulgated for Implementation

A Guangzhou dispatch reports that recently, many in Guangdong's silver industry have been engaged in manipulating finances. On a small scale, this leads to families being bankrupted, and on a larger scale, it affects social finance and disrupts the fiscal system. In recent years, there have been several crises within the silver industry, causing countless victims. The government has been aware of this and has explicitly banned such activities. However, many merchants still harbor hopes of getting away with it and continue to take risks and manipulate things in secret. When Fan Qiwu was the Director of Finance, he once drafted measures to suppress the silver industry, but the Silver Industry Association strongly opposed them, and soon after, Fan left office and the matter was suspended. Now, the Director of Finance, Feng Zhuwan, in order to fundamentally consolidate finances, has specifically added and revised the previously drafted measures, renaming them as Temporary Measures for Managing the Silver Industry. These measures have been submitted to the provincial government for approval. The main points of the measures are as follows: Those engaged in one or more of the following are considered to be in the silver industry: A. Mortgages; B. Savings; C. Deposits and loans; D. Buying and selling raw gold and silver; E. Remittances; F. Currency exchange; G. Bill discounting. Silver businesses are divided into three types: A. Silver firms; B. Exchange shops; C. Money counters. The capital of newly established silver firms should be set at 100,000 yuan or more, and the capital of newly established exchange shops should be set at 10,000 yuan or more. Those with capital of less than 10,000 yuan belong to the category of money counters. The capital of old silver firms should be set at 50,000 yuan or more, and the capital of exchange shops should be set at 5,000 yuan or more. Those with capital of less than 5,000 yuan belong to the category of money counters. Silver firms may engage in all types of business mentioned in these measures, while exchange shops may engage in items E and F mentioned in these measures. Exchange shops may not engage in items A, B, C, and D. Money counters are only allowed to engage in the exchange between silver coins and copper coins, and may not engage in other businesses. All silver firms, exchange shops, or money counters must not purchase waste silver from furnaces. Violators will be dealt with by the Finance Department. All silver firms or exchange shops must submit the name of the store, address, organization, capital amount, business scope, the name and address of the founder, and a list of shareholders to the local business tax agency for transfer to the Finance Department for approval before they can operate. A one-time handling fee of two silver dollars must be paid for the application, and the license must be renewed annually thereafter. Silver firms that also engage in other businesses, or stores that also engage in the silver industry, must divide their capital separately and not mix it. Silver firms or exchange shops may send personnel to the public market to buy and sell, while money counters may not send personnel to the market. All personnel sent to the market to buy and sell must comply with the Silver Industry Market Rules. (January 8)

Hubei Authorities Demand Old Debts from the Central Government 81

The Finance Department Sends Personnel to Beijing to Urge Collection

A Hankou dispatch reports that Hubei Province's finances have long been in a state of exhaustion, and education funding is especially in arrears. The Finance Department has specifically requested the provincial government to demand compensation for old debts from the central government to be stored as a fund. According to the department's calculations, the Hubei Railway Mileage Public Stock amounts to over 800,000 taels of silver. The Ministry of Communications converted the 6% interest public bonds of the third year of the Republic into over 1,159,900 silver dollars, allocated to the Ministry of Finance for special storage, with an annual interest rate of 6%. Over the years, the total outstanding interest amounts to over 891,000 silver dollars, with a total of over 2,051,100 silver dollars in principal and interest. In addition, there is an old debt that was omitted, amounting to over 310,000 taels of silver and over 70,000 silver dollars, which was also converted by the Ministry of Communications into over 511,000 silver dollars, with an annual interest rate of 1%, and it was agreed to repay it in installments, with the repayment period ending at the end of August of the 19th year of the Republic. The deadline has long passed, but no payment has been made. It has been found that the above two amounts have been designated by the provincial government as education funds. Given the current financial difficulties of the provincial treasury, it should be communicated to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Communications to allocate the funds in full for storage. Furthermore, the central government's subsidies for October, November, and December of last year were short by 1,150,000 silver dollars. The Finance Department has also sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, requesting a swift allocation, and has sent Section Chief Gui Jingqiu to Beijing to negotiate. The original request from the Finance Department is recorded as follows: "Since being ordered to abolish the likin tax in January of last year, the finances of this province have suddenly lost a significant source of income. The newly established business tax is insufficient to offset the losses. Since the director of the department took office, he has been in a state of depletion. After considering the situation, he formulated a relief plan, tightening government expenses to reduce expenditures on the one hand, and reorganizing taxes to open up revenue sources on the other. He hoped to implement the plan and remedy the situation. Unexpectedly, last year's floods caused widespread devastation, and the people's difficulties were exacerbated. Revenue could not be increased, and all government affairs were pending. Expenditures could not be reduced, and both old and new taxes were reduced or even non-existent due to the disaster. He was in dire straits, and the only way to make up for the situation was to borrow money, borrowing new to repay old. Then, due to the outbreak of foreign troubles and tight financial conditions, borrowing to make ends meet was difficult to manage, and the old debts accumulated and the new deficits increased. From January to the end of December of last year, the provincial treasury's accumulated deficit reached over 7 million silver dollars. Now, all resources have been exhausted, and he is mentally and physically exhausted. The maintenance costs of various agencies are entirely dependent on the central government's subsidies. The central government's subsidies for the 20th year of the Republic, due to the reorganization of the central government, the remaining balance of 150,000 silver dollars for October and 500,000 silver dollars each for November and December have not been allocated. Revenue is increasingly meager, and expenditures are increasingly difficult. Schools are demanding by striking, and the military and police are blaming the lack of food. The difficult situation is intensifying. The director of the department has been tasked with rescuing the situation, but he has been working day and night without being able to make up for the difficulties. Therefore, he urgently requests that your honorable superior, considering the situation, swiftly allocate the outstanding subsidies of 1,150,000 silver dollars from last year in full, and allocate and remit them monthly in advance to provide relief, so that the current situation can be maintained and provincial affairs will not be paralyzed. The difficult financial situation of Hubei Province, in addition to sending Gui Jingqiu, the section chief of this department, to Beijing to report in person, is presented for your review and implementation with the utmost urgency." (January 11)

The Hunan People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association respectfully proclaims, bearing the official seal."

Banditry in the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Region 83

A Bengbu dispatch reports that the Red bandits in the Henan-Hubei-Anhui border region had few people and guns three years ago, and their strength was very weak. However, due to frequent disasters and the people's lack of livelihood, they took risks, and the communists took the opportunity to instigate them, leading to more and more gatherings. Due to the complex terrain in the Henan-Hubei-Anhui border region, which can be used as a place to come and go and hide, they have nothing to fear, and the bandit flames have become increasingly intense. Although the various armies that have advanced to suppress them have achieved considerable results, the bandits are scattered and reappearing, and after several years, the Red bandits have not been fundamentally eliminated. The areas occupied by the Red bandits are called the Red areas, and the areas stationed by the national army and local militias are called the White areas, demarcating boundaries. Sometimes, due to the balance of power, they do not invade each other. In recent months, due to many incidents in the current situation, the defensive forces have been frequently mobilized, and the bandits have taken the opportunity to seize cities and occupy land, and their momentum has become increasingly rampant. According to those familiar with the bandit situation in the border area, 1. The 7th, 8th, and 9th regiments of the Red bandits are scattered in the Panxin shop and Wanjia shop areas in southern Henan, and one of their forces is still entrenched in the Xuanhua shop bandit nest. 2. The Red bandits in eastern Hubei, Huang'an, who are confronting the 30th Division of Li Mingzhong's troops, are part of the pseudo-13th Division and the pseudo-4th Army. The pseudo-military department and the pseudo-10th Division are stationed in Qiliping. North of Tawan Hill, the 39th regiment of the pseudo-14th Army is stationed. Near Gaojia River and Bali Bay, there is the pseudo-21st Division. Xia shop, Cai shop, Changling Hill, Changcheng Cen and other places are all disturbed by Red Guards. 3. In the Macheng area, there are over a thousand bandits at Tonggu Pass, 7,000 to 8,000 bandits at Changcheng Cen, a Red Guard regiment of over a thousand at Baima Village northwest of Huangtu Hill, a regiment of bandits at Xiajia Bay, and over a thousand Red bandits at Liushudian and Huzi Cen north of Futian River. The more than 10,000 Red bandits who previously attacked Shangcheng have all passed through Guangshan in the south. Bandits frequently disturb the areas of Ma and Huang. 4. Most of the Red bandits in the Jinshui and Guangshui areas are gathered in Moshan and Luotian, attacking and disturbing Meitian, and over 5,000 bandits have fled to Caijia River and Xima, with a tendency to harass Jinshui. Another several thousand Red bandits have attacked Guangji and fled to Caohe Town, also with the appearance of invading Jinshui. 5. The Red bandits on the Anhui border are most rampant in the areas of Huoqiu, Liu'an, Huoshan, and Yingshan. They have been repeatedly suppressed by the Yue Shengxuan department of the garrison army stationed in Liu'an, the Zheng Tingzhen department of the 25th Route Army stationed in Huo, and the Song Shike department of the temporarily compiled 2nd Brigade, but there has been no progress. It is said that there are no less than tens of thousands of bandits entrenched in the areas of Liu, Huo, Ying, and Jinjia Village. This is truly a hidden worry for Anhui Province. (January 12)

Funding for the Grand Canal Project Still Uncertain 85

Disaster Relief Association Suggests Fundraising Methods

The Grand Canal in Jiangbei has been breached in seventeen places since the autumn. Although Ye Chucang, the former chairman of the provincial government, repeatedly guaranteed that it would be repaired in the shortest possible time, it was only after the reorganization of the provincial government that it was learned that only one-tenth of the 4 million yuan stipulated by Ye had been secured, and the rest had been subject to changes in circumstances and remained uncertain. As a result, the hundreds of miles of incomplete canal banks have not been started after five months. Initially, the local area could help raise funds, but with the national crisis at hand, the public's attention has shifted to saving the country. In addition, the starving people in the dozens of counties in Jiangbei are not sure how to get a full meal in this cold weather, and they have no energy to take care of the project. It is now heard that the Huaiyang Water Disaster Relief Association believes that construction is urgently needed, and has formulated six fundraising methods to suggest to the authorities: 1. Please allocate American wheat for disaster relief. 2. Please allocate customs surtax for disaster relief. 3. Please allocate railway surtax for disaster relief. 4. Please allocate the provincial road funds decided by the provincial government. 5. Please allocate the construction mu tax from the counties in Jiangsu Province. 6. Please allocate the land tax from the counties in Jiangbei of Jiangsu Province. It is said that the above methods have been directly presented to the National Government, but it is not yet known whether they will be approved. However, the spring floods will arrive in an instant. If the construction is delayed any longer, the counties upstream will lack water for spring plowing, and the counties downstream will be permanently flooded. At present, the engineering personnel have all been allocated and an engineering office has been set up in the Zhouhuayuan Alley. Han Guojun, the deputy director of the Grand Canal Disaster Relief Association, is currently going to Suzhou, Wuxi, and Shanghai to negotiate everything with charity groups in Jiangnan, so as to make final plans. At the end of the old lunar year, if there is 2 million yuan in cash, construction can begin, otherwise, the disaster may be great, and residents along the canal may not be able to sleep peacefully.

Lifting the Ban on the Nationwide Sale of Soy Sauce 86

The General Inspection Office Has Ordered Its Subordinates to Comply

The nationwide sale of domestic soy sauce has never been subject to regional restrictions. However, in the fifth year of the Republic, salt merchants in western Zhejiang proposed to the Salt Affairs Bureau to establish six rules for soy sauce workshops to purchase salt and sell soy sauce, in order to force the distribution of expensive salt and restrict the sale of soy sauce. Soy sauce made in one place cannot be purchased from another place, and soy sauce made here is not allowed to be sold there. Although this rule is limited to the five districts of Suzhou, it has affected the transportation and sale of soy sauce, and local patrol agencies have repeatedly detained and punished soy sauce. The nationwide sale of soy sauce is no longer possible. As a result, domestic soy sauce cannot go beyond the manufacturing site, but imported foreign soy sauce can be sold nationwide. This is no different from economic suicide, which has aroused the attention of the Chinese people. Therefore, in March of the 19th year of the Republic, the Legislative Yuan proposed relief, and in November of the same year, the National Industrial and Commercial Conference also decided that domestic soy sauce should be allowed to be sold nationwide. The Ministry of Industry issued three notices to the Ministry of Finance, requesting that it be implemented quickly. Last year, the General Inspection Office of the Ministry of Finance's Salt Affairs Bureau, in accordance with the order, took over the national anti-smuggling teams and set up a tax police section to complete the task. However, salt merchants in various places still requested that the transportation and sale of soy sauce be banned, and even pickles were being investigated and banned. The General Inspection Office of the Salt Affairs Bureau believed that soy sauce, according to the current salt law, has been tested and is clearly not a salt and should not be subject to the ban on transportation. Therefore, in December, it requested the Ministry of Finance to clearly instruct and approve the matter. Subsequently, the Ministry of Finance approved it. In January of this year, the General Inspection Office of the Salt Affairs Bureau, in accordance with the Ministry's order, issued a notice to all branch offices and inspection offices, forwarding it to the transport commissioners and salt transport bureau chiefs for information, and ordering their subordinates to comply. In this way, the national soy sauce industry has been relieved of its 15-year-long suffering, and the unnecessary disputes between anti-smuggling agencies and the people can come to an end. The notice from the General Inspection Office of the Salt Affairs Bureau is recorded as follows: "The Regulations on Special Permits for Salt Manufacturing stipulate that any substance containing more than 40% salt content can be regarded as a salt. Soy sauce has been tested and contains only 12.37% salt content, so it is not a salt. However, salt merchants often cite Article 5 of the Rules for Soy Sauce Workshops to Purchase Salt and Sell Soy Sauce in the Five Districts of Suzhou, approved by the Salt Affairs Bureau on December 28 of the 5th year of the Republic, to demand that soy sauce from other districts not be allowed to be sold across borders, and even pickles are requested to be banned, causing frequent disputes and difficulties in handling. Therefore, this office submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance on December 2 of last year, asking whether the cross-border sale of soy sauce, pickles, etc., should be investigated and banned, and requesting clear instructions for compliance. Now, we have received Instruction No. 49736 from the Ministry of Finance on November 22, stating that any substance containing more than 40% salt content can be regarded as a salt. Soy sauce has been tested and contains only 12.37% salt content and should not be regarded as a salt and should not be subject to the ban on transportation. This should be approved. You should immediately forward it for compliance. This order, etc. Having received this, it is hereby copied and issued to all branch offices and offices of this office, ordering them to forward it to all transport commissioners and salt transport bureau chiefs for information, and to order their subordinates to comply."

Local Dispatches 87

Fengxian

The Bandit Alarm in Zhetang Was Found to be a Rumor. For the past few days, society in the county has suddenly spread rumors that a large group of bandits from Taibao Ashu's old troops were entrenched outside Zhetang. The military and police authorities immediately consulted and decided to send troops to suppress them. Yesterday, Chen Jin, the inspector general of the County Public Security Bureau, led a long police force by land and water to patrol and investigate, and the area was found to be peaceful and there were no bandits. However, theft cases have occurred from time to time along the coast. They are small gangs of bandits, and the foreign sea patrol has gone to suppress them.

The Provincial Approval of the Fengnan Boundary Case. In the past, Taiping Township in Nanhui caused a conflict due to boundary demarcation, resulting in the destruction of the residence of He Shiyi, the head of the Nanda Bridge Security Corps. At the same time, Ye Yiyu, the assistant staff member of the district, was also beaten by the people. The dispute between the two sides was very fierce. Fortunately, Shi, Jiang, and Shen Meng of Fengnan County, who were fellow villagers, came forward to mediate. In addition to compensating for various losses, Kong, the magistrate of Nanhui County, also ordered all sectors of the township not to hold meetings or riots before the provincial government had resolved the issue. It is now known that the four townships of Miaoxi and Jinxing, which opposed the merger with Chunxian, are also willing to act in unison with the eleven townships and towns of Nanren Bridge. The township chiefs also jointly telegraphed a petition the other day. According to the approval, the case was presented, and it was found that the Ministry of Internal Affairs had previously approved that the land west of Zha Port in Nanhui County was indeed narrow and long, deviated to the west, and far from Nanhui County, while close to the Fengxian County government. The natural form was not very complete, which was indeed in line with the provisions of Article 7, Item 4 of the Provincial, City, and County Boundary Survey Regulations. It should be strictly investigated and a reorganization method should be proposed and transferred to the Ministry for verification and handling in accordance with the outline of the County Administrative Area Regulations promulgated by the Ministry. The government has ordered the department to comply and verify it.

Songjiang 88

The Ju Surname Robbery Case Solved at the County Level

Concerning a robbery case in this city involving a huge loss of tens of thousands, unprecedented in local history, the city police authorities carried out a search and made an arrest. It is now learned that the suspect, Zhang A'mei, was apprehended twice by Water Patrol Officer Fei Gongxia in early December of last year, and items such as genuine stolen gold and jewelry were confiscated. Just yesterday, these items were presented to the County Government for transfer to the County Court for review and handling. It is reported that the victim, Mo Xiang, yesterday submitted a request to the County Public Security Bureau, stating that all parties involved in the case were relatives and feared implication, requesting that the matter be dropped. It is unknown how the authorities will handle this.

The Constitutional Police Regiment Ordered to Transfer to Hankou

Jiang Qiyuan, the commander of the 5th Constitutional Military Regiment stationed in Songjiang, was originally stationed at the old headquarters. He has now received an order from the Ministry to transfer and garrison in Hankou, to defend the important town. After receiving the order, Commander Jiang immediately led the machine gun company and departed at 6 PM today.

Suzhou 89

Construction of the Ring Road Begins

Qian Tianpeng, Director of the Wuxian Construction Bureau, recently negotiated with the commanders of the 60th Division, Shen, and the two师长(two Division Commanders named Shen), obtaining their approval to dispatch 2,000 soldiers to build the sections of the ring road in the urban area that have not yet been completed. This includes dredging the river sections from Panxu Jiang to Mudu, as well as repairing the Suzhou-Changshu embankment. The City Road Construction Bureau is currently preparing tools and plans to commence work within a week. The budget is expected to be completed within a week. Director Qian has already assigned Section Chief Fan Guangda of the Administrative Section to coordinate with the general affairs, accounting, and all personnel of the administrative section to prepare for the construction work. This section of the road is half of the Suzhou ring road (Provincial Highway Fuhe Road), a crucial link from Changshu Fushan to Jiaxing, Zhejiang. Turning from Nantong, Wujiang, and Jiaxing to Changshu Fushan is an important transportation route. The completion of this road will greatly benefit transportation in the Suzhou area and is of no small significance.

Changshu 90

Continuous Robbery Cases Occur in Dongtang Market

The town of Dongtang, in this county, is located near Yangcheng Lake, and bandit activities are frequent. On the night of the 10th of this month, seven bandit ships arrived at Yangjiazhai in the Goose Farm Township of the area, landing at Qipu Tang. They then successively entered the homes of villagers Yang Xiaotang, Yang [blank], Yang [blank], Yang [blank], and others, engaging in robberies. The total losses are estimated to be over a thousand gold pieces. Afterward, the victims separately reported the incidents to the Third District Office and the First Sub-bureau of the jurisdiction, which in turn reported to superiors for review and handling.

Villagers Mistake Refugees for Bandits

In Hongjia Guanyintang, Shian Township, belonging to the First District of this county, dozens of refugees from other regions arrived at 5 PM on the 12th. After arriving in the town, they, without any explanation, went to people's homes to rob household items. The villagers, unaware of the situation, mistakenly believed them to be bandits and fled in panic. Some even reported the incident to the nearby 14th District Office, which then reported the situation to the First District Office via telephone, which further reported to the joint military-police office, requesting the dispatch of troops. Subsequently, it was reported by the Township Defense Corps that they were refugees, and the Defense Corps escorted them out of the area.

Wuxi 91

A Civil Newspaper Reporter Stabbed in the Dark

Zhu Bingdie, a reporter for the Civil Newspaper, residing outside Guangfu Gate in this county, in the former Taiping Alley, lives in Shangshan Village, District 8 (near the market), and owns hundreds of acres of ancestral farmland. Last winter, Zhu went to the countryside to collect rent, leading to a lawsuit with his paternal uncle, Zhu Meiji, and his wife, Xu. The County Court handled the case. The other day, Zhu went to the home of a Buddhist monk, Yang, near Anzhen, in Wanli, to measure the rent. However, servants Chen Senlin and clerk Wan A'yuan came out to obstruct him, leading to a dispute. Both parties were brought to the 16th Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau, which had jurisdiction over the area. Zhu Meiji then incited his wife, Xu, to go to the bureau to make a scene. Bingdie informed his father-in-law, who scolded Xu. At 9 PM, Zhu and his wife were leaving his father-in-law's house when, in the darkness, Bingdie's right leg was stabbed with an iron weapon, causing a profuse amount of bleeding. He fell to the ground. Yesterday, he was carried to the city to seek examination at the County Court. After examining the injury, Inspector Du ordered an official to confirm the injury. He then instructed Zhu to seek medical treatment and ordered the arrest of the perpetrator.

Gaoyou 92

West Embankment Workers Strike Over Wage Dispute

The post-disaster commission of the Jiangbei Canal Embankment Project previously appointed Yu Heng as the commissioner for rebuilding the west embankment and established an office outside the north gate of this city. The workers were selected by the county governments of the lower five counties from among the disaster-stricken able-bodied men, who were paid 20 copper coins each day by the office for food and 20 copper coins for labor. Currently, the workers are only receiving 10 copper coins for labor, which has been delayed for more than ten days. Yesterday (the 10th) at 1 PM, all the workers, over 400 in number, went on strike together and went to the office to demand that the owed wages be paid at the rate of 20 copper coins. As a result, the office did not acknowledge the issue. The workers had no choice but to accept 10 copper coins each. They are now unwilling to work, and many have returned home. The remaining workers still insist that wages be paid at the original rate, otherwise, they will not return to work.

Pinghu 93

Large Group of Refugees Crossing the Border Causes Disturbance

Yesterday morning, at Paisha outside Xiaonanmen, forty to fifty refugees from various regions arrived, going from house to house demanding food with an aggressive attitude. Upon hearing this, the Public Security Bureau dispatched the chief of the Fourth Sub-bureau, along with police officers, to escort them away. On the same day, a large number of refugees, over a hundred people, also arrived at FuZhen Temple outside the East Gate, seeking overnight accommodation in the village. Zhou Boliang, the chief of the Fifth Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau, fearing that misconduct might occur, led officers through the night to escort them out of the area.

Hangzhou 94

Dispute Over Capturing Fish in West Lake Resolved

The Hangzhou Municipal Government, in order to raise funds for establishing a work-relief center for vagrants, implemented a public auction for fishing rights in West Lake. A merchant, Zhao Danxu, won the bid for four thousand yuan, paying half of the amount upfront and beginning to catch fish. However, less than a week later, Xiong Xiling, Wang Yiting, and others from the Jiangzhe Release Life Association telegraphed the municipal government to stop the practice. They also dispatched Zhong Kanghou of the Municipal Buddhist Association to negotiate compensation with the fish merchant for losses of one thousand five hundred yuan, and transfer all the fish in the lake to Outer Lake for protection.

Xiaoshan 95

Provincial Commissioner Assigned to Recover Old Taxes From Previous Years

Lin, the County Magistrate of Xiaoshan, received an order yesterday from the Provincial Department of Finance stating that the old tax arrears from various counties for the years 1927, 1928, 1929, and 1930, range from tens of thousands to hundreds of thousands of dollars. Among these arrears, there are cases of wealthy households colluding with low-level officials to conceal their assets. The province has assigned [blank] to work with the county bureau chiefs to strictly urge the payment of the arrears, with a deadline of three months. Wealthy households who deliberately delay or refuse payment should be immediately detained according to law. The enforcement must be strict, breaking through any personal connections, especially for the large households.

Provisional General Meeting of Jiangsu Province School Faculty 97

More Than Twenty Representatives from Nineteen Schools Attend

Resolving Fundamental and Temporary Methods for Jiangsu Education Funding

The Entire Body Goes to the Provincial Government, the Education Department, and the Finance Department to Petition

The Jiangsu Provincial United Association of Secondary School Faculty held a provisional representative meeting at the Zhenjiang Provincial High School meeting room at 9 AM on the 11th. Representatives from various schools, including Hu Xia [blank], and more than twenty others, attended. Wu Dezhang presided over the meeting, and Chen Bangxian took the minutes. Concrete opinions were discussed regarding fundamental and temporary methods for provincial funding and collecting debts, totaling eleven proposals. The most important proposal was that the entire body unanimously supported the proposal made by Director Zhou of the Education Department, which was approved by the provincial government on January 8th, to remedy the provincial education funding issue. This entails allocating all income from the Jiangsu Education Fund Management Office to provincial education funding from January of this year onwards. The funding for National Central University will be transferred by the Provincial Government to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Education from the cigarette tax revenues within Jiangsu Province. The representatives were all filled with passionate determination and vowed not to stop until the goal was achieved. Anyone who obstructs this will be regarded as a public enemy of the entire faculty of all schools and should be abandoned by all. At 2 PM that afternoon, the chairman of the association, Wu Dezhang, and others led the entire body to the Education Department to meet Director Zhou and engage in talks for about two hours. They then went to the Provincial Government to meet Chairman Gu. Chairman Gu was away in Shanghai, and the secretary-general was also out on official business. Subsequently, Secretary Ge Jianshi received them. The representatives stated their intentions and requested the chairman to adhere to the end to maintain the fate of Jiangsu education. They then went to the Finance Department to meet Director Shu. Director Shu was away in Shanghai, and all section chiefs and secretaries were attending a meeting to withdraw public bonds at the Chamber of Commerce. The meeting was hosted by the Director of the Second Section. Representative Wu stated that the Finance Department must issue the tens of thousands of dollars owed as soon as possible to relieve the urgent needs. After the petition, everyone returned to their hotels to rest and arranged to take the Nanjing-Wuxi train to the Education Fund Management Office in Nanjing at 9 AM on the 12th to demand payment of the arrears. The association also hoped that the Education Funding Committee and the Education Fund Management Office would be reorganized and that the Management Office would be moved to the provincial capital to facilitate progress. Bad Luck for Football as Malaya Loses All Three Matches 108

British Army Wins 2-1

Winning Goal Scored Through Penalty Kick at the End

The Malayan Overseas Chinese Football Team held the combined Shanghai-based British Army team to a 1-1 draw for eighty minutes at the baseball field yesterday afternoon. Until the last five minutes, after Yu Diao Hua's foul, the British Army's main player, Crankhan, scored a penalty kick to seal a 2-1 victory. The Malayan performance was better than before, but bad luck prevailed. The spectators sighed in regret at Malaya's third defeat in Shanghai. The referee was British Army officer Kailan.

Malayan Lineup 109

Yan Qisheng

Zuo Zhuohua Gan Jinlu Xinde

Huang Jinbai Huang Kehou Xie Jinfu

Xu Jintang Liang Fulai Li Wen

Deng Yueyun

British Army Lineup 110

Baber (Lincoln) Neilans (Medical Corps)

(Military Dentist) Van Nessen (Service Corps) Bolton (Service Corps)

Gleed (Scott) Owen (Service Corps)

Neil (Scott) Crankhan (Lincoln)

Huang Jinbai Still Shows Strong Performance 111

Malaya's performance yesterday was much better than in the previous two matches. They frequently broke through the British Army's defense and probed the enemy's goal. They were not trapped in a corner and constantly surrounded as before. However, although there were many opportunities, they regrettably lost their scoring chances due to inaccurate shots. The center remained the guard, with Huang Jinbai single-handedly taking charge. His performance was still the strongest, saving countless balls. His skill was no less than Zhou Xianyan's. The two goals conceded were both due to his failure to save them.

Crankhan Stands Out From the Crowd 112

The situation on both sides progressed and retreated, which is why the British Army's performance was unremarkable and not surprising. However, Malaya missed countless shots, and the shooting power was unusually weak and unable to score. There were many players from the B team, and their skills were generally less impressive. Only the right-winger, Crankhan, was worth watching. Crankhan was selected for the interport team. His right-wing progress was fast, his passes were accurate, and wherever his traces went, it was as if all the grass and trees were soldiers. The ball that was obtained was dangerous. The British Army's first goal was passed by Crankhan, and the penalty kick was also scored by him, so he was virtually the person who determined Malaya's fate.

Guan Xinde Opens the Scoring First 113

There were only two thousand spectators. Malaya kicked off against the wind, and for only ten minutes there was an attack and retreat. The British Army attacked the goal without success. Liang Fulai passed the ball forward, and Deng Yueyun went straight along the side and passed the ball to Li Wen in the center on the right. Li Wen got the ball and shot, and Smith kicked it out. Deng Yueyun caught it and advanced again. The British left-back Tunna kicked it into a corner kick. Deng fell very accurately. Guan Xinde attacked diagonally and attacked the ball from the goal post and rebounded. Malaya was able to open the scoring.

Redley Heads the Ball Into the Goal 114

The Malayan army was in great spirits and took advantage of the victory to advance. The British Army's defensive line was broken from time to time. Guan Xinde got Yan Qisheng's ball again and shot in front of the goal, but unfortunately the shot was inaccurate. The British Army's right-winger Crankhan also repeatedly harassed, fortunately, without any trouble. After thirty minutes, Owen dribbled the ball and Gan Jinlu stopped him. Crankhan [blank] in the center, and Redley had to head the ball with force, unstoppable and it went in. The score became 1-1, a tie. Although the British army came again, they could no longer enter. The first half ended in a draw.

Twelve-Yard Penalty Leads to Crushing Defeat for Malaya 115

After a break, the British team kicked off and fought hard for forty minutes without a decisive outcome. Moments of great excitement and danger arose repeatedly. Huang Jinbai handled the situation with ease and made no mistakes. Both sides had opportunities but failed to capitalize. Based on the unfolding situation, a draw seemed inevitable. Unexpectedly, in the last five minutes, Crankham attacked from the right, penetrating the penalty area. Yu Zhuohua raised his hand to block the ball, resulting in a handball. Crankham successfully converted the twelve-yard penalty, sealing Malaya's defeat.

Westerners' Football Association Expels the Maotai Team 119

Players Allowed to Join Other Teams

The Executive Committee of the Westerners' Football Association held a meeting on Tuesday evening to discuss the dispute between the Maotai football team and the French Business football team. The following resolutions were made: (1) The Maotai football team is expelled until the end of this year's football season because the team disobeyed orders and refused to continue playing in the Group C match against the French Business team after playing half the game.

(2) All of Maotai's records in Group C are canceled.

The committee's explanation for the above resolutions is as follows: Although Maotai claimed that their refusal to continue playing was due to the French Business team's barbaric actions, according to the report from the referee sent by the Chinese Sports Association, the game was not barbaric. The French Business team did charge several times, which were quite forceful, but legal. Since Maotai did not obey the referee's orders and opinions, the committee had no room for discussion regarding Maotai. However, the expulsion is for the Maotai team, and its players are still allowed to join other teams.

Witty Remarks by Feng Yuxiang 123

— Yi Zang

After experiencing the pain of losing his wife in the tenth year of the Republic, Feng remarried a Miss Li from Tongzhou, Beijing. Miss Li graduated from Yenching University in Beijing. She was virtuous and proficient in English. After marrying Feng, she raised his orphaned children and managed his affairs in an orderly manner. Therefore, Feng favored her greatly. Because Feng did not understand English, his wife taught him English every morning, while he taught Li military strategy and party principles. The couple diligently learned from each other without regard to the weather. Feng was a firm believer in Sun Yat-sen's teachings. When he was the Northwestern Border Defense Commissioner, his house was filled with books on the Three Principles of the People. Besides reading them himself, he also encouraged his subordinates to do so. Xu, an old scholar, lived in Feng's house. Every evening, he would lecture Feng and his wife on the Book of Changes, the Book of Rites, and the Spring and Autumn Annals. They studied late into the night, year after year. Therefore, all those close to Feng envied their marital harmony.

Feng usually walked to his office in the new village. The office had several cars for long-distance travel. One day, his eldest son secretly took a car for a joyride. Feng happened to be going out on business. Upon learning of the situation, Feng grabbed a stick and went straight out. The son got out of the car. Feng beat him severely. His limbs were almost crippled. Zhang Zhijiang, Xiong Bin, and others rushed to intercede. However, Feng, in his rage, was difficult to persuade. Soon, his wife, Miss Li, also arrived. Seeing her son's injuries, she was filled with grief and cried out, "Even if he is completely wrong, should there be no affection at all? If something goes wrong, this son is not mine, and as a stepmother, I will not only be criticized by the world but also be accused of indifference. What about my reputation?" After saying this, she knelt on the ground, asking Feng to strike her instead. Only then did Feng's anger subside slightly. However, after returning home, Feng ordered his orderly to escort his son to the Zhangjiakou Arsenal, ordering him to learn blacksmithing. The factory director treated the son with great respect, not making him work, and settling him in an inner room. Unexpectedly, Feng secretly investigated the next day. Seeing his son living comfortably in the inner room, he was furious, scolding the factory director for shielding and concealing. The factory director had no excuse. Feng then forcibly dragged his son to the iron smelting yard, forcing him to do blacksmithing work, and fined the factory director three months' salary.

World Anecdotes 124

— Hai Ke

The New Wonders of Traveling the World: The latest wonders that we are happy to praise are five men and three women traveling the world in strange ways. One is wearing roller skates, and three are walking entirely on foot. One girl works as a waitress in each country she visits. And another woman travels while spinning a hula hoop. These unique ways of traveling are truly fascinating. The one traveling on roller skates is named James Stevens.

He left New York in the United States six months ago. He will soon arrive in the UK. When he left, he had no money. Along the way, he only did odd jobs to make a living. The girl who works exclusively as a waitress is a 22-year-old London student. She hopes to write a book about her experiences. She is currently in Russia and will not return home for two years. The woman traveling and spinning a hula hoop is the wife of an unemployed man. She has three children and a heavy burden. Someone bet her that she could not do it. She refused to accept it and set off without a penny. She has already completed three-quarters of the journey and is still energetic and not tired. Another person, a 14-year-old boy named Jack Oldham, and his father are traveling around the world in a tandem bicycle. They left London eight months ago and are now in Japan. They teach people how to play the lute to support themselves. Another woman traveling around the world is Miss Marjorie Gilruth. She joined a small ship as an ordinary sailor. She gets up at 5:30 every morning and does the work of a sailor. She sometimes even steers the ship. She is extremely hardworking. Her goal is to travel around the world.

Nine-Nine Cold Dispelling Chart 125

— Liu Zhongyang

I once saw a Nine-Nine Cold Dispelling Chart in the home of a Manchu friend in Beijing. It was said to have been passed down from the palace. It evoked images of palace ladies, talented and idle, expressing their feelings with poems on red leaves floating down the palace moat. The chart consists of nine characters (庭前楊柳珍重待春風 - 'The willows in the courtyard are cherished, awaiting the spring breeze') calligraphed in thin strokes on a foot-long scroll to be hung on the wall. It predates the calendar. The characters are outlined in double strokes, with the interior left blank for filling in. The winter solstice is the start of the nine-nine period, totaling eighty-one days. These nine characters have nine strokes each, totaling eighty-one strokes. Starting from the first day of the nine-nine period, one stroke is filled in each day. Each time a character is filled, it indicates that one nine-day period has passed. When all nine characters are filled, it indicates that the nine-nine period has ended and spring has returned. The meaning of these nine characters is both excellent and auspicious. If colored drawings of pavilions and willows are added to enhance it, it would make a wonderful adornment for a lady's boudoir or study.

Since the September 18th Incident, the entire nation has been filled with indignation. However, I believe that revenge and redress are not matters that can be accomplished overnight. We must persevere to succeed. In particular, the entire nation must be united, and everyone must have the spirit of taking the redress of shame as their own responsibility. The reason why the enemy country can unite its people to plot against us is also because they have been inducing and rewarding aggressive thoughts in the minds of every student since early childhood education, irrigating and nurturing them, not just for a day. Our country has suffered many national humiliations, but the Twenty-One Demands are the most significant. Therefore, I have imitated the Nine-Nine Cold Dispelling Chart and created a National Humiliation Chart to hang in my study, so that it will be a shocking sight. The chart uses the double-stroke method to outline the two characters (國恥 - National Humiliation) on a large piece of paper. Each character is a foot in size. Because the two characters for National Humiliation have exactly twenty-one strokes, I will write one clause of the Twenty-One Demands in each stroke, according to the order of the treaty and the sequence of the strokes. If a clause is cancelled in the future, I will fill in that stroke. It must be filled in before it can be removed. I believe that the education authorities could adopt this idea, modify it, and create a more perfect National Humiliation Chart to be distributed to schools across the country and hung in classrooms. Teachers can use the chart to remind students not to forget the national humiliation before starting each lesson. It is similar to how King Fuchai of Wu had someone stand in the courtyard and shout, reminding him not to forget the revenge of Yue.

Going on Expedition 126

— A Member of the Youth Aid-Horse Team

(11) Arrival in Xuzhou

On the twenty-eighth, after we said goodbye to our compatriots in the capital, we took a boat to Pukou. At this time, the gentle waves were rippling. Our bodies floated up and down with the boat, which was very interesting. I unconsciously thought I was inside a warship. The gray clouds of sorrow seemed like the smoke of the battlefield. Everything outside the boat seemed like the enemy. Therefore, my spirit became more and more vigorous and courageous. But these were all illusions. The shouts of the Zhuangshi of Tientai killing the enemy seemed to be ringing in my ears: "Ah, move forward!" It was really exhausting. My body was still in a safe area. When will I be able to sacrifice myself for the country?

A Letter Regarding Recent Artistic Trends in Paris (Middle) 127

— Liu Kang

My teacher's selected snow scene is displayed in Room 14, in a very good position. Sheng's seascape is hung in Room 10, which is also not bad. Prince Yun, who calls himself the only exhibitor, also occupies a position near the stairs, painting a panoramic view of the Concorde. Zhang Chengjiang sent two sculptures, both of which were displayed, giving a boost to the Chinese sculpture world, which is gratifying.

More than twenty Japanese artists are exhibiting, which is noteworthy. Although there are few works of extraordinary genius, their hard work and perseverance are admirable.

Mrs. Besnard held an exhibition of her late husband's works, including dozens of watercolors and sculptures, with the sculptures being more refined.

The decoration and architecture departments have many surprising things. In short, the word "new" is the root of the strangeness.

Music, fashion, and dance performances are held every day or two. This year's dance is particularly wonderful. All the Danseurs and Danseuses are invited from the Paris Opera and the Berlin Opera.

French cuisine is boasted by the French as the best in the world. They spare no effort in promoting research. There are cooking museums, exhibitions, and lectures for people to refer to and observe, in order to achieve perfection. Recently, it has been listed as the eighth art form and officially participates in various art Salons. This autumn exhibition has a separate department dedicated to the display or performance of cooking techniques, which is one example. The general situation of the autumn exhibition is as described above. Now, I will tell you a few recent events in Paris: The world economic panic has affected the development of industry and commerce. Therefore, the number of unemployed people is increasing day by day. The so-called unemployed people generally refer to workers, vendors, etc. But I don't know that there are also unemployed people in the intellectual class, such as school teachers, stage actors, musicians, and painters, sculptors, writers, etc., who are all telling each other about the difficulty of making a living. Unemployed workers in England and Germany have what is called unemployment insurance. When they have nothing to do, they can receive some living expenses from the government to maintain their survival. In France, the national construction plan for 1932 has also been announced recently, with the aim of accommodating unemployed workers and enabling them to have work and earn money. Only the unemployed in the upper classes are not considered, which inevitably loses the essence of freedom, equality, and fraternity. The French government, in view of this, has specially organized an art (limited to painters and sculptors) unemployment relief association, with the sole purpose of subsidizing or relieving unemployed painters and sculptors. The honorary presidents, French President Doumer and Prime Minister Laval, have agreed to serve. There are six committee members, including your friend A. Pesmard, a member of the National Academy, and the rest are heads of various art groups and celebrities in the art world.

We departed from Pukou. We passed through Chuxian, Bengbu, and Suxian in Anhui. We stayed for a short time along the way. On the morning of the thirty-first, we finally arrived at Tongshan Prefecture (Xuzhou) in Jiangsu Province. The compatriots here are very enthusiastic about patriotism. They had already been waiting for us at the station. A welcome meeting was also held in the public education hall. After the meeting, the whole group paraded through the city. All the participating groups also joined in. There were many spectators along the way, silently moved to tears.

The scenery here is magnificent. The mountains are structured like a screen. The mountainsides are inlaid with sparse silver piles. One or two green old pine trees stand out in the leafless and flowerless withered bushes, seeming to express their spirit of perseverance. This is a model for our passionate youth.

The soil in Xuzhou is not fertile. Therefore, the citizens are also very poor and commerce is not very developed. Recently, it has also been affected by floods, making it even more desolate. Arriving here, the north wind is very strong. It is indeed not as comfortable as Jiangnan. However, we feel more and more pleased because our destination is getting closer.

Miss Yunlan 128

— Piao Ran

Tianyi Film Company's latest Movietone production has already started filming. The plot of the film is sad and beautiful. It depicts a woman with an extremely gentle disposition who allows fate to control her life, with no power to resist. Because she does not dare to resist her family, she sacrifices her affectionate companion and marries a man she does not know. Fortunately, that man is also a gentle and affectionate young man. Therefore, she also enjoys a lot of family happiness. A year later, she even became a mother. But the god of fate came to tease her again. She suddenly met her former lover. Because of an unfounded suspicion, she was kicked out by her in-laws and returned to her mother's home. Her family would not take her in. Then, she complied with the demands of her former lover and lived with him. Although life was poor, they were still sweet. Later, he could not stand the pressure of life and left this world. Naturally, she fell into a more miserable situation. She felt that there was no one she could be close to in this vast world. Suddenly, an idea came to her mind. She thought of her son. So she went to her ex-husband's house to secretly see her child. Taking advantage of people's carelessness, she picked him up and ran away. Finally, they discovered her and chased her out. As a result, she was run over by a train. The film is directed by Shao Zuiweng and stars Chen Yumei. The title of the film has been set as "Miss Yunlan." Chen is a star who is good at playing tragic roles. With her starring in this film, the excellence of the future results can be imagined.

— Master of the Seeking Happiness Studio

Since she has disappeared like a cloud in the sky, with no indication whatsoever, he can only reflect on himself. Another Decrease of Five Taels and Six Mace. Yesterday, the gold price initially showed stability but then weakened, with fluctuations throughout the day totaling ten taels. Initially, there was a slight increase, but the big players saw that the rise would not materialize and instead witnessed a slight fall. Subsequently, buyers became active, and interest briefly broke through 690 taels. However, due to the unstable situation, sellers were emboldened, and the market fell back into weakness, ultimately closing at 682-683 taels.

Foreign Exchange: British Flat, American Loose 131

One US Dollar Equals Three Taels, Zero Mace, Seven Fen, Six Li, Nine Hao, Two Si of Silver.

Yesterday, British silver fell slightly, while American silver rose instead. Market conditions remained flat with no new developments. The United States was in a wait-and-see mode. However, the exchange rate suddenly rose, with the British against the US dollar at 3 yuan, 4 jiao, 1 fen, and 2.5 li, and the US dollar against the British at 3 yuan, 4 jiao, 0 fen, and 8.7 li. As for the HSBC quotation, British gold increased by one-two-five (1.25) to 1 shilling and 11 pence, and the US dollar added .375 to 32.5 yuan, with Hong Kong adding 1.25 to 76 taels and 25%. The domestic market saw British silver flat and American silver loose, due to the exchange rate. Initially flat, then strong, then frustrated, the noon closing turned flat. As a result, British gold did not see glory or disgrace compared to the previous day, and the US dollar rose slightly by 1.25. Discount Rate Soars 133

Customs Duty Retention Certificates Trading Suspended

Peak Reaches Seven Mace and Three Fen

Market Overview. Yesterday morning, the market did not show any changes, and the overall trend remained calm. Then, news of the retention of customs duties and salt taxes spread throughout the city. The securities exchange was the first to be affected, and trading was immediately suspended. The financial sector suffered significant losses in the storage of various securities. The banking industry, in particular, suffered a major blow to its ready cash reserves for banknote preparation. Therefore, the banks rushed to the market to collect cash for preparation in the afternoon. Unexpectedly, there were too many monks and not enough gruel, and the supply could not meet the demand. As a result, the discount rate skyrocketed, extending the trading time until 3 pm, more than an hour longer than usual. The price reached a peak of seven mace and three fen, a new and unprecedented change.

Discount Rates. The "foreign" morning discount rate was slightly lower than the previous afternoon by three hao and seven hu, half, at seven qian, one fen, five li, one hao, two hu, half. The market suddenly changed, opening at over seven qian and two fen, with the highest quote reaching seven qian and two fen, and the difference between buying and selling reaching two to three million, making it impossible to close. Fortunately, the Bank of China and the Central Bank maintained the sale of more than two hundred thousand before finally managing to pass. The discount rate suddenly increased by four to five li, reaching seven qian and two fen, a very tense situation. The "silver" discount rate was not as urgent in the morning market, but in the afternoon market, although there was no emergency, it was already more urgent. Banks did not post rates, and the water was added to five or six fen.

Subsidiary Coin Market Situation. The Jiangnan small silver dollar was 6 qian, 5 fen, 7 li and a half in both the morning and afternoon markets, with a morning trade of 5,000 jiao and an afternoon trade of 6,000 jiao. The Guangdong small silver dollar was 6 qian, 5 fen, 7 li, 7 hao and a half in the morning market, and also increased by more than two li in the afternoon market, calculated at 6 qian, 6 fen. The morning trade was 125,000 jiao and the afternoon trade was 50,000 jiao. Copper coins remained at 372,000 wen.

It is estimated that Chinese and foreign banks received and settled more than 7 million, with Chinese merchants receiving and settling more than 1.8 million in notes, foreign merchants receiving and settling more than 1.3 million in notes, and various goods, foreign exchange taxes, and miscellaneous amounts totaling more than 10 million. The Seriousness of the Bond Market is Worth Paying Attention To 134

The Securities Exchange Suspends New Trading, No Market

Silver and Money Industries Meet Yesterday to Discuss Maintenance Methods

Regarding our country's domestic national bonds, ever since the invasion of Northeast China by Japanese troops last year and last month, the situation has been unstable and prices have fallen sharply. Although there have been rallies in the interim, the overall market trend has been deteriorating and declining. Despite repeated efforts to maintain it, it has been difficult to reverse the decline. Moreover, the environment in the bond market has become even worse recently. According to recent newspaper reports, the northern and southern provinces and regions have retained national taxes, and the future of the fund is directly and significantly pressured. The bond fund custodian has been working hard on this rescue and has telegraphed various parties to seek maintenance. It is hoped that the central government and various provinces and regions will be able to take into account the interests of the people and properly address the aftermath, so as not to endanger the future. The Securities Exchange, in view of the unfavorable environmental situation, has announced the suspension of new futures trading for safety reasons. The brokers have decided to suspend trading temporarily, which can properly address and rescue the silver and money industries. The bond market is also very concerned about this and has held a meeting to discuss rescue measures. Therefore, whether or not the Securities Exchange will open for trading today depends on the situation of all parties. According to broker sources, all parties are now very concerned about the issue of fund custody.

Sun Fo and Others Returned to Beijing Yesterday 149

Feng Yuxiang and Li Jishen Were Also Traveling Together

Zou Lu Discusses Diplomacy, Deeming it Never Possible to Settle Harmoniously

As the President of the Executive Yuan, Sun Fo, expressed his active responsibility, the situation improved slightly. Yesterday morning at 9:45, all the remaining Central Committee members in Shanghai took a train to Beijing together. The travelers included Feng Yuxiang, Sun Fo, Chen Youren, Li Jishen, Chen Mingshu, Wu Tiecheng, Li Wenfan, Ma Chaojun, Ye Gongchuo, and Zeng Zhongming. Deng Jiayan, Liang Hancao, Wen Jiangang, Chen Qun, Chen Jianru, Zhong Tianxin, Tang Yueliang, and Fu Bingchang also accompanied them.

Departure from Shanghai: The Railway Bureau specially prepared two flower-decorated cars and one first-class car attached to the express train for the ministers to ride. The pilot train departed at 9:10. Railway police and the 19th Route Army maintained order both inside and outside the station, with strict precautions. Wu Tiecheng and Chen Mingshu arrived first around 9:00. At 9:20, Sun Fo, along with Feng Yuxiang, Li Wenfan, Li Jishen, and Ye Gongchuo, arrived and boarded the train together. Those who came to see them off included Zhang Zhijiang and Guo Chengen. The train departed at 9:50.

Chen Mingshu's Remarks: Chen Mingshu told reporters upon boarding the train that the diplomatic situation was urgent and the central government lacked leadership. Because Mr. Chiang and Mr. Wang and Mr. Hu were not able to immediately go to Beijing to preside over the major plans, it was decided at the Central Political Council to set up a special committee to deal with the national crisis. However, the establishment of the committee and its organization, etc., must be further considered and decided after arriving in Beijing.

Feng Yuxiang's Remarks: According to Mr. Feng Yuxiang, he was invited to Beijing by Mr. Zhenru to be nominated as one of the members of the special committee. He said that he would do everything in his power to serve the country. The date of going to Hong Kong or Fengtian would be decided after returning to Shanghai in the near future.

Students' Request: Before the train departed, four student representatives from secondary schools in Hangzhou requested to meet with Sun Fo, the President of the Executive Yuan. Wu Tiecheng, the Mayor of Shanghai, and Chen Mingshu, the Vice President, met with them outside the train. The students requested subsidies for travel expenses when petitioning in Fenghua and Hong Kong. As a result, the Mayor of Shanghai agreed to the request for Fenghua and gave them a note to see Secretary-General Yu of the Municipal Government. Regarding the travel expenses for Hong Kong, Vice President Chen instructed the students to send a telegram to him (Chen himself) after he arrived in Beijing, and it would be handled.

Zou Lu's Conversation: Yesterday, a reporter met with Central Committee member Mr. Bi Haibin at his private residence. The conversation was as follows: Reporter (asked): Today (i.e., yesterday morning), all the Central Committee members have returned to Beijing. Is your staying in Shanghai because you will go to Hong Kong? (Answer): It is not yet decided whether I will go. (Asked): In your opinion, will Hu Zhantang be able to respond to the Central Committee's urging to come north this time? (Answer): I'm afraid he will not come. (Asked): Besides deciding on the special committee, was there any other discussion when you attended the meeting at Sun's residence the day before yesterday? (Answer): The issues of finance and diplomacy were also discussed. The meeting lasted a long time. (Asked): Can you tell us about the results of the plan? (Answer): These two issues are of great importance and cannot be released temporarily. They must be publicly announced after the central government makes a decision. As for the general situation: (1) Diplomacy will take a tough approach, neither compromising nor adopting a policy of non-resistance. (2) There are already solutions for finance, but the specific solutions must be temporarily delayed. (Asked): What are your opinions on the issue of provinces intercepting tax revenues, and are there any solutions? (Answer): The interception of tax revenues by the provinces is not a problem. Since the provinces intercept tax revenues and do not remit them, they will be responsible for the military, political, and educational expenses of the province. The central government can maintain itself with the direct tax revenue it receives. (Asked): What are your opinions on the party affairs disputes, and how will they be resolved? (Answer): Now we need to come up with proper solutions for government finance and diplomacy before discussing the party's problems. (Asked): Is it true that the party affairs will be reorganized? (Answer): The previous party was too bureaucratic, so reorganization may be inevitable. At this point, Mr. Zou excused himself because he had another appointment.

Huang Hanliang and Lin Kanghou Resign as Minister and Vice Minister of Finance 150

Their Resignations Were Submitted Yesterday

Huang Hanliang, the acting Minister of Finance, had just taken office on New Year's Day and came to Shanghai to plan for military and political expenses. Yesterday, he suddenly submitted his resignation. Lin Kanghou, the Permanent Vice Minister of Finance, had not yet taken office and also requested to withdraw his appointment. It has been learned that the two men's resignations are as follows:

Huang Hanliang's Memorial to the National Government: A memorial stating the reason for requesting permission to resign due to insufficient capacity. I, Hanliang, was ordered to act as the Minister of Finance, and I know that I am mediocre and not fit for the position. However, due to the current national crisis, I am carrying out the government's wishes, fulfilling the duty of a commoner, and reluctantly taking on the arduous task, hoping to remedy the national finances. However, after more than ten days in office, I realized that it would be difficult to achieve any of the plans. The division of national treasury revenue is worrying. With my limited ability, I cannot reverse this trend. If I continue to force myself, I will mislead the overall situation. It is better to give way to someone more capable as soon as possible to reduce guilt. Therefore, I am submitting this memorial to request permission to resign as acting Minister of Finance. I respectfully request your review and approval.

Lin Kanghou's Memorial to the Executive Yuan: A memorial stating the reason for requesting the withdrawal of the appointment due to inability to assist with departmental affairs. I, Kanghou, was ordered to act as the Permanent Vice Minister of Finance. As a citizen, I dared not avoid national affairs. Therefore, in my private capacity, I have been planning departmental affairs with acting Minister Huang and conspiring with the financial community to improve the national financial plan, hoping to contribute my modest efforts. However, I have only felt that my heart is willing but my strength is insufficient, and I have been unable to assist. I should not hold an empty title and obstruct the path of the capable. Therefore, I am submitting this memorial to request the withdrawal of the appointment as acting Permanent Vice Minister of Finance. I humbly request your approval.

Opposition From All Sectors to the Suspension of Principal and Interest Payments on Public Bonds 151

The Shanghai Customs 2.5% Surtax National Treasury Bond Fund Custody Committee, the Bankers' Association, the Money Trade Association, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce have issued declarations and telegrams in opposition to the central government's proposed misappropriation of funds. These are recorded separately below:

Fund Custody Committee 152

Declaration: The Shanghai Customs 2.5% Surtax National Treasury Bond Fund Custody Committee issued a declaration yesterday stating that since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, it first issued the Shanghai Customs 2.5% Surtax National Treasury Bond and established this committee to be publicly elected by social organizations to be custodian of the principal and interest fund for this bond. Article 5 of the Custody Regulations stipulates that (before the principal and interest of this bond are fully repaid, the scope of its custodianship shall not be changed). Article 8 stipulates that the Shanghai Customs revenue of 2.5% surtax should be notified by the Finance Committee to the collecting agency, which should allocate the full amount collected to the Fund Committee on a daily basis from the designated date. Subsequently, the National Government continued to issue this bond four times: Cigarette Tax National Treasury Bond, Post-Settlement Short-Term Public Bond, 17th Year Financial Short-Term Public Bond, 17th Year Financial Long-Term Public Bond, Second Disaster Relief Public Bond, Disarmament Public Bond, Second Customs Short-Term National Treasury Bond, Post-Settlement Short-Term National Treasury Bond, Compilation of National Treasury Bonds Customs Public Bond, Unified Tax National Treasury Bond, Salt Tax National Treasury Bond, and 20th Year Financial Public Bond, etc., all of which were entrusted to this Committee for custody in accordance with the principles stipulated in the above regulations by the Ministry of Finance of the National Government. This Committee bears the heavy trust of the people and the power granted by the state. We vow to do our best to protect the national credit and the rights of the people. For several years, we have never defaulted. However, recently we heard that the central government has proposed to misappropriate the fund, causing unrest in the market. If this becomes a reality, the bonds will be no different from waste paper. The impact will affect the life and death of people throughout the country. It is the duty of this Committee to do everything possible and adopt various measures to ensure that the regulations of the National Government continue to be effective. We also hope that everyone will work together to make up for our shortcomings. This is a special declaration for your public knowledge.

Telegram to the National Government: To Chairman Lin of the National Government, President Sun of the Executive Yuan, and Vice President Chen: We have recently heard that the government intends to misappropriate the funds of public bonds and treasury bonds, causing panic among the people and shaking the market. Since the establishment of the National Government, financial personnel have repeatedly come up with ways to raise domestic debt to provide financial support. The public bonds and treasury bonds issued over the years have reached more than 900 million yuan. The reason why these bonds can circulate in the market and regulate finance is that the principal and interest have never been defaulted on, thus maintaining the people's trust. If the principal and interest payments are suspended, they will immediately become waste paper. The government's credit will be swept away, and economic panic will arise. The people will suffer the tragedy of national economic bankruptcy, and the government will also lose the financial resources to rescue finance. This policy of killing the chicken to get the egg is extremely harmful to both the country and the people. With the wisdom of the government officials, they should not resort to such a strategy. Moreover, President Sun of the Executive Yuan stated in an interview with reporters on January 5 that he would do his best to maintain credit by paying the principal and interest of various public bonds on schedule to avoid disturbing the financial system. Minister Huang of Finance also stated in his inaugural declaration that the public bond fund should be strictly maintained to ensure financial security and strengthen bond credit. How could they go back on their words so quickly? If there is such a proposal, please resolutely abandon it and make a clear announcement to reassure the people. This Committee bears the heavy trust of the government and the people. In order to maintain the government's credit and protect the people's rights, we must do everything possible and adopt various measures to ensure that the bond regulations remain effective. It is our duty to not remain silent. We offer this loyal advice and hope you will consider it carefully.

Bondholders' Association 153

The National Association of Public Debt Bondholders issued a declaration yesterday stating that in recent years, the state's political expenses have been excessively expanded, and various new taxes have been implemented in succession, which are still not enough to meet its needs. Therefore, public bonds and treasury bonds have been issued several times a year in succession, and the total amount has reached no less than 700 to 800 million yuan. If the subscriptions are not sufficient, they are followed by compulsory distribution and tax collection (this phenomenon existed when the Changguan and goods taxes in various places were not abolished). Therefore, our country's public bonds have a phenomenon that is absolutely different from other countries, that is, the government does not consider the needs of the market and the ability of the people to bear it when issuing them, but only if it is necessary to maintain political expenses, it will not hesitate to order the people to subscribe to all the sources necessary for their livelihood. Therefore, the people's livelihood and bond credit have become interlinked. If credit can be maintained and the principal and interest are repaid annually, the people holding bonds can still receive interest or use it to circulate in the market to support their lives. Otherwise, if the principal and interest are suspended, holding bonds is tantamount to waste paper. These 700 to 800 million yuan of bonds are scattered among the people, which is equivalent to 700 to 800 million yuan of property. Once they lose their effectiveness, it is tantamount to the simultaneous bankruptcy of the people across the country. Over the years, although the government's treasury has been extremely exhausted, it has never defaulted on the repayment of principal and interest on a monthly basis, and it knows the importance of this and dare not quench thirst with poison and seek temporary pleasure. It is unexpected that at the beginning of the cooperation between Ning and Guangdong and the establishment of the new government, there is suddenly a proposal to suspend the payment of principal and interest on all domestic debts. This kind of action is tantamount to announcing the confiscation of the property prepared by the people over the years, destroying the people's livelihood, and destroying the country's credit. On the one hand, it ignores the retention of tax revenue, redundant troops, and wasteful expenses, resulting in the failure of finance, and has no choice but to plunder the sources of the people's livelihood to temporarily subsidize political expenses. This kind of measure only inspires the ambition of tax interceptors and supports the extravagant. The people of the country should rise up and oppose it to the death in order to establish the country's economic position. Based on the above-mentioned purpose, this association has set up an office at Xinyichang Securities No. 5 on the 80th floor of Edward VII Avenue, and is also borrowing a meeting place from the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to regularly handle bond registration. It is hoped that bondholders across the country will unite and actively participate in jointly maintaining bond credit. This is a special declaration.

Bankers' Association and Money Trade Association 154

The various public bonds and treasury bonds issued by the National Government over the years are large in number, and what is shown to the people is nothing more than a solid fund, strong credit, and repayment of principal and interest in accordance with the regulations, without any defaults. Our people support the country and are willing to buy bonds with their hard-earned money, using them as education funds, charity funds, daily living expenses, or business operations. They rely on the principal and interest of the bonds. Once the fund is shaken, panic will arise, and the impact will be felt throughout the country. You, the pillars of the party and the state, care about the people's livelihood and should not commit suicide and plunge the people into bankruptcy. Moreover, President Huang has repeatedly declared at the beginning of his tenure that he will do his best to maintain the public bond fund, which is related to the country's credit. How could he forget his words? Please make a clear statement to dispel the doubts of the people.
